2. **RSI is extremely low (13.5)** – while this can precede a short‑term bounce, it also reflects strong selling pressure that may continue.
3. **Volatility is high (~10 %)**, giving the potential for a 5‑10 % move in either direction within the next few hours.
4. **Technical and short scores (>0.6)** align with a short bias, but the momentum score (0.70) hints at a possible short‑term rebound.
5. **Support at 0.037258** is close; a break below could open the path to further downside toward the next support zone.

### Potential Trade Thesis
- **Primary idea:** Initiate a short position near the current price (0.0400) with a tight stop just above the recent high or near the pivot (≈ 0.0467) to limit loss to ~1 % of entry.
- **Target:** Aim for the identified support (≈ 0.0373) and possibly further down to the lower Bollinger band (~0.0317), delivering a 5‑10 % move, satisfying the required ≥3.6 % TP for asymmetric payoff.
- **Risk/Reward:** Entry 0.0400, stop ~0.0465 (≈ 16 % risk), target 0.0373 (≈ 6.8 % reward) – not enough R:R. To meet the 3:1 target, tighten stop to ~0.0420 (≈ 5 % risk) and keep target at 0.0373 (≈ 12 % reward), achieving ~2.4:1. Consider extending target to 0.0317 for a ~20 % reward, achieving >3:1 R:R.

- **Function Called:** `blofin_get_funding_rate`  
- **Instrument:** `TAC-USDT` (TAC perpetual futures against USDT)

**Funding Data**

| Field | Value | Interpretation |
|-------|-------|----------------|
| `fundingRate` (raw string) | `"0.00006989543801233511"` | ≈ **0.00699 %** per funding interval |
| `funding_rate` (numeric) | `6.989543801233511e-05` | Same as above, expressed as a decimal |
| `fundingTime` | `"1782964800000"` | Unix‑ms timestamp → **2026‑07‑02 03:00 UTC** (next funding event) |
| `bias` | `"neutral"` | No strong long‑or‑short pressure from funding |
| `sentiment_score` | `0.5` | Mid‑point on a 0‑1 scale, confirming neutral stance |
| `note` | `"Funding near neutral."` | Plain‑language summary |

**Key Insights for Trading Decision**

1. **Neutral Funding Bias** – The funding rate is very small and close to zero, indicating that longs and shorts are paying roughly the same amount. There is no clear directional edge from funding cost/benefit.

2. **Magnitude** – At ~0.007 % per funding period, the cost (or credit) is negligible for short‑term positions. It will not materially affect profit‑and‑loss for a typical intraday or swing trade.

3. **Timing** – The next funding timestamp is **2026‑07‑02 03:00 UTC**. If you hold a position through that time, the tiny rate will be applied, but the impact remains minimal.

**Potential Action**

- Since funding does not provide a decisive bias, rely on **price‑action, volume, and other technical indicators** to determine entry/exit for `TAC-USDT`. Funding can be ignored for now, but keep monitoring it for any future shift away from neutral.

| **low24h** | `0.3598` | Lowest price in the last 24 h |
| **volCurrency24h** | `4,933,012` | 24‑hour volume expressed in USDT |
| **vol24h** | `4,933,012` | 24‑hour volume expressed in base currency (WLD) – appears to be a duplicate of the USDT volume, likely a data‑feed quirk |
| **ts** | `1782941663925` | Timestamp (ms since epoch) – corresponds to **Sat, 01 May 2025 22:34:23 UTC** (note: timestamp seems stale; verify current market data) |
| **chg_pct** | `-9.584%` | Price change over the last 24 h (down ~9.6 %) |

### Key Insights
- **Current price** is around **$0.3698** per WLD, essentially flat between bid and ask.
- **Liquidity** is healthy: >24 k WLD on the ask side and >8 k on the bid side at the top level.
- **24‑hour range**: $0.3598 – $0.4193, a **≈13 %** swing, indicating moderate volatility.
- **Downward pressure**: price is down **~9.6 %** from the 24‑hour open, suggesting bearish momentum in the last day.
- **Volume** is sizable (~$5 M), providing sufficient market depth for sizable trades.

### Potential Issues / Flags
- The timestamp (`ts`) is from **May 2025**, not the current date (July 2026). This suggests the API returned **stale data**. Verify with a fresh request before making any trading decisions.
- `volCurrency24h` and `vol24h` are identical; normally they represent different units (quote vs base). Treat the volume figure as approximate.

**Recommendation:** Re‑query `blofin_get_ticker` (or another live market data source) to obtain up‑to‑date price, volume, and timestamp before proceeding with any analysis or trade planning.
